class="overflow-y-auto p-4" dir="ltr"><code class="!whitespace-pre language-python"><span><span>connection = connection.starttls()
</span></span></code></div></div></pre>
<p data-start="96" data-end="350" class=""><code data-start="96" data-end="108">starttls()</code> does <strong data-start="114" data-end="121">not</strong> return a new connection; it just upgrades the existing connection. When you assign <code data-start="205" data-end="241">connection = connection.starttls()</code>, you overwrite your SMTP connection with <code data-start="283" data-end="289">None</code>, which causes the <code data-start="308" data-end="324">AttributeError</code> when calling <code data-start="338" data-end="347">login()</code>.</p>
<h3 data-start="352" data-end="372" class="">✅ <strong data-start="358" data-end="372">Fixed Code</strong></h3>

<h3 data-start="1719" data-end="1751" class="">🔥 <strong data-start="1726" data-end="1751">Fixes &amp; Improvements:</strong></h3>
<ol data-start="1752" data-end="2015">
<li data-start="1752" data-end="1819" class="">
<p data-start="1755" data-end="1819" class=""><strong data-start="1755" data-end="1783">Fixed <code data-start="1763" data-end="1775">starttls()</code> Issue</strong> – No longer reassigns <code data-start="1806" data-end="1818">connection</code>.</p>
</li>
<li data-start="1820" data-end="1930" class="">
<p data-start="1823" data-end="1930" class=""><strong data-start="1823" data-end="1871">Used <code data-start="1830" data-end="1843">os.getenv()</code> Instead of <code data-start="1855" data-end="1869">os.environ[]</code></strong> – Avoids <code data-start="1881" data-end="1891">KeyError</code> if an environment variable is missing.</p>
</li>
<li data-start="1931" data-end="2015" class="">
<p data-start="1934" data-end="2015" class=""><strong data-start="1934" data-end="1989">Added Debugging <code data-start="1952" data-end="1987">print("Email sent successfully!")</code></strong> – Confirms email is sent.</p>
</li>
</ol>

</div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></article><article class="w-full text-token-text-primary" dir="auto" data-testid="conversation-turn-12" data-scroll-anchor="false"><h6 class="sr-only">ChatGPT said:</h6><div class="text-base my-auto mx-auto py-5 px-6"><div class="mx-auto flex flex-1 text-base gap-4 md:gap-5 lg:gap-6 md:max-w-3xl group/turn-messages focus-visible:outline-none" tabindex="-1"><div class="group/conversation-turn relative flex w-full min-w-0 flex-col agent-turn @xs/thread:px-0 @sm/thread:px-1.5 @md/thread:px-4"><div class="relative flex-col gap-1 md:gap-3"><div class="flex max-w-full flex-col flex-grow"><div data-message-author-role="assistant" data-message-id="f80e6478-91a7-4bdc-9a8f-a59619b7e544" dir="auto" class="min-h-8 text-message relative flex w-full flex-col items-end gap-2 whitespace-normal break-words text-start [.text-message+&amp;]:mt-5" data-message-model-slug="gpt-4o"><div class="flex w-full flex-col gap-1 empty:hidden first:pt-[3px]"><div class="markdown prose w-full break-words dark:prose-invert light"><p data-start="0" data-end="216" class="">You're facing an <code data-start="17" data-end="55">SMTPAuthenticationError (535, 5.7.8)</code> error, which means that Gmail is rejecting your username and password. This happens because Google considers less secure apps a risk and blocks them by default.</p>
<hr data-start="218" data-end="221" class="">
<h3 data-start="223" data-end="268" class="">✅ <strong data-start="229" data-end="268">Fixes for SMTP Authentication Error</strong></h3>
<h4 data-start="269" data-end="314" class=""><strong data-start="274" data-end="314">1. Use an App Password (Recommended)</strong></h4>
<p data-start="315" data-end="418" class="">Since Gmail blocks regular passwords for SMTP authentication, you need to generate an <strong data-start="401" data-end="417">App Password</strong>:</p>
<ol data-start="420" data-end="694">
<li data-start="420" data-end="495" class="">
<p data-start="423" data-end="495" class="">Go to <a data-start="429" data-end="494" rel="noopener" target="_new" class="">Google App Passwords</a>.</p>
</li>
<li data-start="496" data-end="568" class="">
<p data-start="499" data-end="568" class="">Select <strong data-start="506" data-end="516">"Mail"</strong> as the app and <strong data-start="532" data-end="552">"Other (Custom)"</strong> for the device.</p>
</li>
<li data-start="569" data-end="609" class="">
<p data-start="572" data-end="609" class="">Generate a 16-character App Password.</p>
</li>
<li data-start="610" data-end="694" class="">
<p data-start="613" data-end="694" class="">Use this generated password instead of your regular Gmail password in the script.</p>
</li>
</ol>
<p data-start="696" data-end="720" class="">Update your <code data-start="708" data-end="714">.env</code> file:</p>

<h4 data-start="1386" data-end="1439" class=""><strong data-start="1391" data-end="1439">3. Enable Less Secure Apps (Not Recommended)</strong></h4>
<p data-start="1440" data-end="1523" class="">If you <strong data-start="1447" data-end="1475">cannot use App Passwords</strong>, you must allow <strong data-start="1492" data-end="1512">Less Secure Apps</strong> in Google:</p>
<ol data-start="1524" data-end="1666">
<li data-start="1524" data-end="1597" class="">
<p data-start="1527" data-end="1597" class="">Go to <a data-start="1533" data-end="1596" rel="noopener" target="_new" class="">Less Secure Apps</a>.</p>
</li>
<li data-start="1598" data-end="1666" class="">
<p data-start="1601" data-end="1666" class="">Turn it <strong data-start="1609" data-end="1615">ON</strong> (Google may disable this setting after some time).</p>
</li>
</ol>
<p data-start="1668" data-end="1756" class="">⚠️ <strong data-start="1671" data-end="1680">Note:</strong> Google is phasing out this option, so it's better to use <strong data-start="1738" data-end="1755">App Passwords</strong>.</p>
<hr data-start="1758" data-end="1761" class="">
<h4 data-start="1763" data-end="1826" class=""><strong data-start="1768" data-end="1826">4. Enable 2-Step Verification (If Using App Passwords)</strong></h4>
<p data-start="1827" data-end="1918" class="">If you have <strong data-start="1839" data-end="1870">2-Step Verification enabled</strong>, you <strong data-start="1876" data-end="1884">must</strong> use an <strong data-start="1892" data-end="1908">App Password</strong> (Step 1).</p>
<hr data-start="1920" data-end="1923" class="">
<h3 data-start="1925" data-end="1947" class="">🔥 <strong data-start="1932" data-end="1947">Final Steps</strong></h3>
<ol data-start="1948" data-end="2050">
<li data-start="1948" data-end="1980" class="">
<p data-start="1951" data-end="1980" class="">Generate an <strong data-start="1963" data-end="1979">App Password</strong>.</p>
</li>
<li data-start="1981" data-end="2024" class="">
<p data-start="1984" data-end="2024" class="">Update <code data-start="1991" data-end="1997">.env</code> with the <strong data-start="2007" data-end="2023">App Password</strong>.</p>
</li>
<li data-start="2025" data-end="2050" class="">
<p data-start="2028" data-end="2050" class="">Run your script again!</p>
</li>

import requests
import smtplib
import os
from dotenv import load_dotenv

load_dotenv()


practice_url = "https://appbrewery.github.io/instant_pot/"
live_url = "https://www.amazon.com/dp/B075CYMYK6?psc=1&amp;ref_=cm_sw_r_cp_ud_ct_FM9M699VKHTT47YD50Q6"

response = requests.get(practice_url, headers ={"accept-language":"en-US"})

soup = BeautifulSoup(response.content,"html.parser")


price = soup.find(class_ ="a-offscreen").get_text()

price_without_currency =price.split("$")[1]

price_as_float =float(price_without_currency)
print(price_as_float)

title = soup.find(id="productTitle").getText().strip()
print(title)

buy_price = 100
if price_as_float &lt; buy_price:
    message =f"{title} is on sale {price}!"

    with smtplib.SMTP(os.environ["SMTP_ADDRESS"],port=587) as connection:
        connection =connection.starttls()
        result = connection.login(os.environ["EMAIL_ADDRESS"], os.environ["EMAIL_PASSWORD"])
        connection.sendmail(
            from_addr = os.environ["EMAIL_ADDRESS"],

<p data-start="165" data-end="180" class="">🔴 <strong data-start="168" data-end="178">Issue:</strong></p>
<ul data-start="181" data-end="433">
<li data-start="181" data-end="277" class="">
<p data-start="183" data-end="277" class=""><code data-start="183" data-end="195">starttls()</code> <strong data-start="196" data-end="232">does not return a new connection</strong>. It just upgrades the existing connection.</p>
</li>
<li data-start="278" data-end="433" class="">
<p data-start="280" data-end="433" class="">When you reassign <code data-start="298" data-end="334">connection = connection.starttls()</code>, you overwrite your connection with <code data-start="371" data-end="377">None</code> (or a tuple), causing the error when calling <code data-start="423" data-end="432">login()</code>.</p>
</li>
</ul>
<hr data-start="435" data-end="438" class="">

✅ <strong data-start="2053" data-end="2075">Used <code data-start="2060" data-end="2073">os.getenv()</code></strong> – Avoids <code data-start="2085" data-end="2095">KeyError</code> if variables are missing.<br data-start="2121" data-end="2124">

<li data-start="1122" data-end="1162" class="">
<p data-start="1124" data-end="1162" class=""><strong data-start="1124" data-end="1138">Yahoo Mail</strong> → <code data-start="1141" data-end="1162">smtp.mail.yahoo.com</code></p>
</li>

    connection.starttls()  </span><span><span class="hljs-comment"># Secure connection</span></span><span>
    connection.login(EMAIL_ADDRESS, EMAIL_PASSWORD)  </span><span><span class="hljs-comment"># Authenticate</span></span><span>
    connection.sendmail(
        from_addr=EMAIL_ADDRESS,
        to_addrs=EMAIL_ADDRESS,
        msg=</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"Subject: Amazon Price Alert!\n\nYour product is on sale!"</span></span><span>
    )

</span><span><span class="hljs-built_in">print</span></span><span>(</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"✅ Email sent successfully!"</span></span><span>)
</span></span></code></div></div></pre>

<h3 data-start="189" data-end="223" class="">🔴 <strong data-start="196" data-end="223">Possible Causes &amp; Fixes</strong></h3>
<h4 data-start="224" data-end="265" class="">✅ <strong data-start="231" data-end="265">1. Use an App Password (Gmail)</strong></h4>
<p data-start="266" data-end="384" class="">If you're using Gmail, <strong data-start="289" data-end="335">you cannot use your regular email password</strong>. Instead, you must generate an <strong data-start="367" data-end="383">App Password</strong>:</p>

<h2 data-start="206" data-end="242" class="">✅ <strong data-start="211" data-end="242">Fix This Error Step by Step</strong></h2>
<h3 data-start="243" data-end="295" class="">1️⃣ <strong data-start="251" data-end="295">Use an App Password (Required for Gmail)</strong></h3>
<p data-start="296" data-end="401" class="">Gmail <strong data-start="302" data-end="337">does NOT allow normal passwords</strong> for third-party apps. You must use an <strong data-start="376" data-end="392">App Password</strong> instead.</p>
<h4 data-start="403" data-end="452" class="">🔹 <strong data-start="411" data-end="452">How to Generate a Gmail App Password:</strong></h4>
<ol data-start="453" data-end="957">
<li data-start="453" data-end="576" class="">
<p data-start="456" data-end="576" class="">Open <strong data-start="461" data-end="488">Google Account Security</strong>:<br data-start="489" data-end="492">
👉 <a data-start="498" data-end="576" rel="noopener" target="_new" class="">https://myaccount.google.com/security</a></p>
</li>
<li data-start="577" data-end="722" class="">
<p data-start="580" data-end="722" class="">Scroll down to <strong data-start="595" data-end="614">"App Passwords"</strong> (under "Signing in to Google").<br data-start="646" data-end="649">
🔸 If you don’t see this option, enable <strong data-start="692" data-end="715">2-Step Verification</strong> first.</p>
</li>
<li data-start="723" data-end="766" class="">
<p data-start="726" data-end="766" class="">Click <strong data-start="732" data-end="764">"Select App" → Choose "Mail"</strong></p>
</li>
<li data-start="767" data-end="825" class="">
<p data-start="770" data-end="825" class="">Click <strong data-start="776" data-end="823">"Select Device" → Choose "Windows Computer"</strong></p>
</li>
<li data-start="826" data-end="891" class="">
<p data-start="829" data-end="891" class="">Click <strong data-start="835" data-end="849">"Generate"</strong>, and <strong data-start="855" data-end="889">copy the 16-character password</strong></p>
</li>
<li data-start="892" data-end="957" class="">
<p data-start="895" data-end="957" class="">Replace your <code data-start="908" data-end="914">.env</code> file’s password with the new App Password.</p>
</li>
</ol>

from bs4 import BeautifulSoup
import spotipy
from spotipy.oauth2 import SpotifyOAuth

date = input("which year do you want to travel to?Type the data in this format YYYY-MM-DD")
url ="https://www.billboard.com/charts/hot-100/2000-08-12/"

#spotify authenication

<h3 data-start="2320" data-end="2344" class="">🔥 <strong data-start="2327" data-end="2344">What's Fixed?</strong></h3>
<p data-start="2345" data-end="2679" class="">✅ <strong data-start="2347" data-end="2384">Uses the input <code data-start="2364" data-end="2370">date</code> dynamically</strong> in the Billboard URL.<br data-start="2406" data-end="2409">
✅ <strong data-start="2411" data-end="2452">Hides <code data-start="2419" data-end="2430">client_id</code> and <code data-start="2435" data-end="2450">client_secret</code></strong> using <code data-start="2459" data-end="2465">.env</code> file.<br data-start="2471" data-end="2474">
✅ <strong data-start="2476" data-end="2510">Fixes the Spotify search query</strong> (<code data-start="2512" data-end="2538">track:{song} year:{year}</code>).<br data-start="2540" data-end="2543">
✅ <strong data-start="2545" data-end="2579">Creates the playlist only once</strong> (not inside the loop).<br data-start="2602" data-end="2605" data-is-only-node="">
✅ <strong data-start="2607" data-end="2641">Handles missing songs properly</strong> (skips songs not found on Spotify).</p>

class="min-h-8 text-message relative flex w-full flex-col items-end gap-2 whitespace-normal break-words text-start [.text-message+&amp;]:mt-5"><div class="w-full"><div class="flex w-full flex-col import requests
from bs4 import BeautifulSoup
import spotipy
from spotipy.oauth2 import SpotifyOAuth

date = input("which year do you want to travel to?Type the data in this format YYYY-MM-DD")
url =f"https://www.billboard.com/charts/hot-100/{date}/" 

header = {"User-Agent": "Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 10.0; Win64; x64; rv:131.0) Gecko/20100101 Firefox/131.0"}
response = requests.get(url=url,headers=header)
spotify_page = response.text

soup = BeautifulSoup(spotify_page,"html.parser")
song_name_spans = soup.select("li ul li h3")
song_name =[song.getText().strip() for song in song_name_spans]

#spotify authenication
sp = spotipy.Spotify( 
        auth_manager = SpotifyOAuth(
        scope= "playlist-modify-private",
        redirect_uri = "http://example.com",
        client_id = os.getenv("client_id"),
        client_secret =  os.getenv("client_secret")
        show_dialog= True,
        cache_path ="token.txt",
        
        )
)

user_id = sp.current_user()["id"]

print(user_id)




song_URIs =[]
year = date.split("-")[0]
for song in song_name:
    result = sp.search(q=f"track:{song} year:{year}",type="track")
    print(result)
    try:
        uri =result['tracks']["items"][0]["uri"]
        song_URIs.append(uri)
    except IndexError:
        print(f"{song} doesn't exist in spotify. skipped ")

        playlist=sp.user_playlist_create(user=user_id,name=f"{date} Billboard 100",public=False)
        print(f"playlist created:{playlist['name']}")

        if song_URIs:
           sp.playlist_add_items(playlist_id=playlist["id"], items=song_URIs)
           print("Songs added to the playlist.")
        else:
           print("No songs were found to add.")</div></div></div></div></div></div><div class="flex absolute left-0 right-0 flex justify-end"><div class="-me-1 -ms-2.5 flex select-none items-center import requests
from bs4 import BeautifulSoup
import spotipy
from spotipy.oauth2 import SpotifyOAuth

date = input("which year do you want to travel to?Type the data in this format YYYY-MM-DD")
url =f"https://www.billboard.com/charts/hot-100/{date}/" 

header = {"User-Agent": "Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 10.0; Win64; x64; rv:131.0) Gecko/20100101 Firefox/131.0"}
response = requests.get(url=url,headers=header)
spotify_page = response.text

soup = BeautifulSoup(spotify_page,"html.parser")
song_name_spans = soup.select("li ul li h3")
song_name =[song.getText().strip() for song in song_name_spans]

#spotify authenication
sp = spotipy.Spotify( 
        auth_manager = SpotifyOAuth(
        scope= "playlist-modify-private",
        redirect_uri = "http://example.com",
        client_id = os.getenv("spotipy_client_id"),
        client_secret =  os.getenv("spotipy_client_secret"),
        show_dialog= True,
        cache_path ="token.txt",
        
        )
)

user_id = sp.current_user()["id"]

print(user_id)




song_URIs =[]
year = date.split("-")[0]
for song in song_name:
    result = sp.search(q=f"track:{song} year:{year}",type="track")
    print(result)
    try:
        uri =result['tracks']["items"][0]["uri"]
        song_URIs.append(uri)
    except IndexError:
        print(f"{song} doesn't exist in spotify. skipped ")

        playlist=sp.user_playlist_create(user=user_id,name=f"{date} Billboard 100",public=False)
        print(f"playlist created:{playlist['name']}")

        if song_URIs:
           sp.playlist_add_items(playlist_id=playlist["id"], items=song_URIs)
           print("Songs added to the playlist.")
        else:
           print("No songs were found to add.")</div></div></div></div></div></div><div class="flex absolute left-0 right-0 flex justify-end"><div class="-me-1 -ms-2.5 flex select-none items-center class="relative flex min-h-0 flex-auto flex-grow flex-col"><div class="react-scroll-to-bottom--css-zyqwp-79elbk h-full"><div class="react-scroll-to-bottom--css-zyqwp-1n7m0yu flex flex-col"><div id="prosemirror-context-children"></div><div class="relative z-10 flex max-w-full h-fit" id="prosemirror-editor-container" style="padding-bottom: 1rem;"><div class="_main_5jn6z_1 z-10 markdown prose contain-inline-size dark:prose-invert focus:outline-none bg-transparent ProseMirror" contenteditable="false" style="width: 775px;" translate="no"><h1><span>Spotify Playlist Creator from Billboard Hot 100</span></h1><h2><span>Description</span></h2><p><span>This Python script scrapes the Billboard Hot 100 chart for a given date and creates a Spotify playlist with the top songs from that date. It utilizes </span><span><strong>BeautifulSoup</strong></span><span> for web scraping and </span><span><strong>Spotipy</strong></span><span> for Spotify API authentication and playlist creation.</span></p><h2><span>Prerequisites</span></h2><p><span>Ensure you have Python installed on your system and set up a virtual environment if needed.</span></p><h3><span>Install Required Libraries</span></h3><p><span>Run the following command to install the necessary dependencies:</span></p><div class="cm-editor ͼ1 ͼ3 ͼ4 ͼ1o ͼ3a" data-is-code-block-view="true" contenteditable="false"><div class="cm-announced" aria-live="polite"></div><div tabindex="-1" class="cm-scroller"><div spellcheck="false" autocorrect="off" autocapitalize="off" translate="no" contenteditable="true" class="cm-content" role="textbox" aria-multiline="true" style="tab-size: 4;"><div class="cm-line">pip install requests beautifulsoup4 spotipy python-dotenv</div></div><div class="cm-layer cm-layer-above cm-cursorLayer" aria-hidden="true" style="z-index: 150; animation-duration: 1200ms;"><div class="cm-cursor cm-cursor-primary" style="left: 6px; top: 5.6001px; height: 18.3999px;"></div></div><div class="cm-layer cm-selectionLayer" aria-hidden="true" style="z-index: -2;"></div></div></div><h2><span>Setup Instructions</span></h2><h3><span>1. Set Up Spotify API Credentials</span></h3><ul data-spread="false"><li><p><span>Create a Spotify Developer Account at </span><span><a disabled="true">Spotify Developer Dashboard</a></span></p></li><li><p><span>Create a new application and note down the </span><code><span>Client ID</span></code><span> and </span><code><span>Client Secret</span></code></p></li><li><p><span>Set up a </span><span><strong>redirect URI</strong></span><span> (e.g., </span><code><span>http://example.com</span></code><span>)</span></p></li></ul><h3><span>2. Create a </span><code><span>.env</span></code><span> File</span></h3><p><span>Create a </span><code><span>.env</span></code><span> file in the project directory and add the following:</span></p><div class="cm-editor ͼ1 ͼ3 ͼ4 ͼ1o ͼ3b" data-is-code-block-view="true" contenteditable="false"><div class="cm-announced" aria-live="polite"></div><div tabindex="-1" class="cm-scroller"><div spellcheck="false" autocorrect="off" autocapitalize="off" translate="no" contenteditable="true" class="cm-content" role="textbox" aria-multiline="true" style="tab-size: 4;"><div class="cm-line">SPOTIPY_CLIENT_ID=your_client_id</div><div class="cm-line">SPOTIPY_CLIENT_SECRET=your_client_secret</div><div class="cm-line">SPOTIPY_REDIRECT_URI=http://example.com</div></div><div class="cm-layer cm-layer-above cm-cursorLayer" aria-hidden="true" style="z-index: 150; animation-duration: 1200ms;"><div class="cm-cursor cm-cursor-primary" style="left: 6px; top: 5.59998px; height: 18.4px;"></div></div><div class="cm-layer cm-selectionLayer" aria-hidden="true" style="z-index: -2;"></div></div></div><h3><span>3. Run the Script</span></h3><p><span>Execute the script using:</span></p><div class="cm-editor ͼ1 ͼ3 ͼ4 ͼ1o ͼ3c" data-is-code-block-view="true" contenteditable="false"><div class="cm-announced" aria-live="polite"></div><div tabindex="-1" class="cm-scroller"><div spellcheck="false" autocorrect="off" autocapitalize="off" translate="no" contenteditable="true" class="cm-content" role="textbox" aria-multiline="true" style="tab-size: 4;"><div class="cm-line">python main.py</div></div><div class="cm-layer cm-layer-above cm-cursorLayer" aria-hidden="true" style="z-index: 150; animation-duration: 1200ms;"><div class="cm-cursor cm-cursor-primary" style="left: 6px; top: 5.59998px; height: 18.4px;"></div></div><div class="cm-layer cm-selectionLayer" aria-hidden="true" style="z-index: -2;"></div></div></div><p><span>Enter a date in </span><code><span>YYYY-MM-DD</span></code><span> format when prompted.</span></p><h2><span>Uploading to GitHub</span></h2><h3><span>1. Initialize a Git Repository</span></h3><p><span>Run the following commands to set up a new Git repository:</span></p><div class="cm-editor ͼ1 ͼ3 ͼ4 ͼ1o ͼ3d" data-is-code-block-view="true" contenteditable="false"><div class="cm-announced" aria-live="polite"></div><div tabindex="-1" class="cm-scroller"><div spellcheck="false" autocorrect="off" autocapitalize="off" translate="no" contenteditable="true" class="cm-content" role="textbox" aria-multiline="true" style="tab-size: 4;"><div class="cm-line">git init</div><div class="cm-line">git add .</div><div class="cm-line">git commit -m "Initial commit"</div></div><div class="cm-layer cm-layer-above cm-cursorLayer" aria-hidden="true" style="z-index: 150; animation-duration: 1200ms;"><div class="cm-cursor cm-cursor-primary" style="left: 6px; top: 5.59998px; height: 18.4px;"></div></div><div class="cm-layer cm-selectionLayer" aria-hidden="true" style="z-index: -2;"></div></div></div><h3><span>2. Create a New GitHub Repository</span></h3><ul data-spread="false"><li><p><span>Go to </span><span><a disabled="true">GitHub</a></span><span> and create a new repository.</span></p></li><li><p><span>Copy the repository URL.</span></p></li></ul><h3><span>3. Push Your Code to GitHub</span></h3><p><span>Replace </span><code><span>your-repo-url</span></code><span> with your actual repository URL:</span></p><div class="cm-editor ͼ1 ͼ3 ͼ4 ͼ1o ͼ3e" data-is-code-block-view="true" contenteditable="false"><div class="cm-announced" aria-live="polite"></div><div tabindex="-1" class="cm-scroller"><div spellcheck="false" autocorrect="off" autocapitalize="off" translate="no" contenteditable="true" class="cm-content" role="textbox" aria-multiline="true" style="tab-size: 4;"><div class="cm-line">git remote add origin your-repo-url</div><div class="cm-line">git branch -M main</div><div class="cm-line">git push -u origin main</div></div><div class="cm-layer cm-layer-above cm-cursorLayer" aria-hidden="true" style="z-index: 150; animation-duration: 1200ms;"><div class="cm-cursor cm-cursor-primary" style="left: 6px; top: 5.6001px; height: 18.3999px;"></div></div><div class="cm-layer cm-selectionLayer" aria-hidden="true" style="z-index: -2;"></div></div></div><h2><span>Troubleshooting</span></h2><h3><span>1. Empty Song List</span></h3><ul data-spread="false"><li><p><span>Billboard might have changed its website structure. Inspect the site manually and update the </span><code><span>soup.select()</span></code><span> query accordingly.</span></p></li><li><p><span>Check if your requests are being blocked by adding appropriate headers.</span></p></li></ul><h3><span>2. Spotify Authentication Errors</span></h3><ul data-spread="false"><li><p><span>Ensure your </span><span><strong>client ID and secret</strong></span><span> are correct.</span></p></li><li><p><span>Make sure you've set up the </span><code><span>.env</span></code><span> file properly.</span></p></li></ul><h2><span>Future Improvements</span></h2><ul data-spread="false"><li><p><span>Handle request blocks using </span><code><span>selenium</span></code><span> or </span><code><span>scrapy</span></code></p></li><li><p><span>Add support for multiple charts (e.g., Top 200, Global)</span></p></li><li><p><span>Improve error handling and logging</span></p></li></ul><p><br class="ProseMirror-trailingBreak"></p></div><div class="pointer-events-none relative flex h-full flex-shrink-0 z-20 basis-0" style="width: 0px; opacity: 1; will-change: auto;"><div class="pointer-events-auto absolute bottom-0 left-0 top-0 w-0 overflow-visible pl-2"></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></main></section></div><div class="absolute bottom-0 z-20 h-24 w-full transition-colors" style="height: 4em; background: linear-gradient(rgba(255, 255, 255, 0), rgb(255, 255, 255));"></div></div></div><button class="flex min-h-5 w-fit select-none pt-[3px] text-start text-token-text-secondary hover:text-token-text-primary">Edited</button></div></div><div data-message-author-role="assistant" data-message-id="35f94c93-d9aa-4a85-840e-a47dfc9b6910" dir="auto" class="min-h-8 text-message relative flex w-full flex-col items-end gap-2 whitespace-normal break-words text-start [.text-message+&amp;]:mt-5" data-message-model-slug="gpt-4o"><div class="flex w-full flex-col gap-1 empty:hidden first:pt-[3px]"><div class="markdown prose w-full break-words dark:prose-invert light"><p data-start="0" data-end="144" class="">I've updated your README file to include instructions for uploading the project to GitHub. <h3 data-start="508" data-end="554" class=""><strong data-start="512" data-end="552">4. Create a New Repository on GitHub</strong></h3>
<ul data-start="555" data-end="826">
<li data-start="555" data-end="592" class="">
<p data-start="557" data-end="592" class="">Go to <a data-start="563" data-end="592" rel="noopener" target="_new" class="" href="https://github.com/">GitHub</a></p>
</li>
<li data-start="593" data-end="622" class="">
<p data-start="595" data-end="622" class="">Click on <strong data-start="604" data-end="622">New Repository</strong></p>
</li>
<li data-start="623" data-end="671" class="">
<p data-start="625" data-end="671" class="">Name your repository (e.g., <code data-start="653" data-end="670">spotify-scraper</code>)</p>
</li>
<li data-start="672" data-end="738" class="">
<p data-start="674" data-end="738" class=""><strong data-start="674" data-end="684">Do not</strong> initialize with a README (since you already have one)</p>
</li>
<li data-start="739" data-end="826" class="">
<p data-start="741" data-end="826" class="">Copy the repository URL (e.g., <code data-start="772" data-end="825">https://github.com/yourusername/spotify-scraper.git</code>)</p>
</li>
</ul>

<h3 data-start="1158" data-end="1187" class=""><strong data-start="1162" data-end="1185">7. Verify on GitHub</strong></h3>
<p data-start="1188" data-end="1273" class="">Go to your GitHub repository and refresh the page—you should see your files uploaded.</p>
<hr data-start="1275" data-end="1278" class="">

Here's a step-by-step guide to push your project to GitHub:</p>
<h3 data-start="73" data-end="110" class="">1. <strong data-start="80" data-end="110">Create a GitHub Repository</strong></h3>
<ul data-start="111" data-end="338">
<li data-start="111" data-end="148" class="" style="">
<p data-start="113" data-end="148" class="">Go to <a data-start="119" data-end="148" rel="noopener" target="_new" class="" href="https://github.com/">GitHub</a></p>
</li>
<li data-start="149" data-end="215" class="" style="">
<p data-start="151" data-end="215" class="">Click on the <strong data-start="164" data-end="171">"+"</strong> (top-right) and select <strong data-start="195" data-end="215">"New repository"</strong></p>
</li>
<li data-start="216" data-end="267" class="" style="">
<p data-start="218" data-end="267" class="">Give it a name (e.g., <code data-start="240" data-end="266">spotify-playlist-scraper</code>)</p>
</li>
<li data-start="268" data-end="306" class="" style="">
<p data-start="270" data-end="306" class="">Choose <strong data-start="277" data-end="289">"Public"</strong> or <strong data-start="293" data-end="306">"Private"</strong></p>
</li>
<li data-start="307" data-end="338" class="" style="">
<p data-start="309" data-end="338" class="">Click <strong data-start="315" data-end="338">"Create repository"</strong></p>
</li>
</ul>
<h3 data-start="340" data-end="381" class="">2. <strong data-start="347" data-end="381">Initialize Git in Your Project</strong></h3>
<p data-start="382" data-end="457" class="">Open your terminal (or command prompt) and navigate to your project folder:</p>
